210000={
	name=Cairne
	dynasty=116000
	dna="aiamhamhfok"
	culture=tauren religion=earth_mother_worship
	martial=8 diplomacy=7 stewardship=7 intrigue=3 learning=6
	add_trait=misguided_warrior add_trait=robust add_trait=strong
	disallow_random_traits = yes
	father=210089 #Voarn
	# Died at 107 in 613 year
	505.9.26={ birth=yes add_trait=creature_tauren }
	536.1.1={
		add_trait=diligent
		add_trait=brave
		add_trait=just
		add_trait=class_warrior_7
		remove_trait=misguided_warrior
		add_trait=skilled_tactician
		add_trait=defensive_leader
		
		add_spouse=210002
		effect={
			add_lover=210002
		}
	}
	603.5.10={
		effect={
			add_friend=10021 #Go'el/Thrall
			add_friend=68001 #Vol'jin
		}
	}
	605.5.20={
		wealth = 300 #Military budget
	}
	610.1.1={ death=yes}
}
